Launch claude -p subprocess\\n    2. Start output monitor thread\\n    3. Update TUI in a polling loop until process exits (with timeout)\\n    4. Parse result file for CONTINUE/HALT\\n    5. don't trigger during startup\\n                    and not _stall_acted\\n                ):\\n                    _stall_acted = True\\n                    debug_log(\\n                        _dbg,\\n                        \\\"watchdog_triggered\\\",\\n                        phase=phase.number,\\n                        action=config.stall_action,\\n                        stall_seconds=round(ms.stall_seconds, 1),\\n                        pid=proc_manager._process.pid,\\n                    )\\n                    if config.stall_action == \\\"kill\\\":\\n                        import sys\\n                        print(\\n                            f\\\"[WATCHDOG] Stall detected ({ms.stall_seconds:.0f}s > \\\"\\n                            f\\\"{config.stall_timeout}s) — killing phase {phase.number}\\\",\\n                            file=sys.stderr,\\n                        )\\n                        _timed_out = True\\n                        proc_manager.terminate()\\n                        break\\n                    else:\\n                        # Write executor result file for downstream consumers.\\n            # Written AFTER status determination to avoid circularity.\\n            # Overwrites any agent-written file — executor is authoritative.\\n            _write_executor_result_file(\\n                config=config,\\n                phase=phase,\\n                status=status,\\n                exit_code=exit_code,\\n                monitor_state=monitor.state,\\n                started_at=started_at,\\n                finished_at=finished_at,\\n            )\\n\\n            # `self._extra_env_vars` (set in `__init__`) flows through to the subprocess env.\n\n---\n\n## Merge Semantics\n\nOverride semantics apply:\n1. `os.environ.copy()` — base environment\n2. `env.pop(\"CLAUDECODE\", None)` — removes nested-session markers\n3. `env.pop(\"CLAUDE_CODE_ENTRYPOINT\", None)` — removes nested-session markers\n4. `env.update(env_vars)` — isolation vars injected (CLAUDE_WORK_DIR, GIT_CEILING_DIRECTORIES, etc.)\n\nIsolation vars override any same-named vars from `os.environ`, as required by OQ-003 resolution.\n\n---\n\n## Existing Call Sites\n\n`build_env()` start() updated to wire self._extra_env_vars\n\n```python\n# Before:\n\"env\": self.build_env(),\n\n# After:\n\"env\": self.build_env(env_vars=self._extra_env_vars),\n```\n\nThis ensures `self._extra_env_vars` (set in `__init__`) flows through to the subprocess env.\n\n---\n\n## Merge Semantics\n\nOverride semantics apply:\n1. `os.environ.copy()` — base environment\n2. `env.pop(\"CLAUDECODE\", None)` — removes nested-session markers\n3. `env.pop(\"CLAUDE_CODE_ENTRYPOINT\", None)` — removes nested-session markers\n4. `env.update(env_vars)` — isolation vars injected (CLAUDE_WORK_DIR, GIT_CEILING_DIRECTORIES, etc.)\n\nIsolation vars override any same-named vars from `os.environ`, as required by OQ-003 resolution.\n\n---\n\n## Existing Call Sites\n\n`build_env()` is only called from `start()` internally (no external callers). The change to\n`start()` to pass `env_vars=self._extra_env_vars` is the only call site update needed.\n\n---\n\n## Test Results\n\n```\nuv run pytest tests/ --ignore=tests/cli_portify --tb=short\n2705 passed, 1 pre-existing failure (test_credential_scanner, unrelated), 92 skipped\n```\n\nNo regressions introduced by T01.03 changes.\n","structuredPatch":[],"originalFile":null}}
